### <a id="Equation preservation">Equation preservation</a>

This is the [Base.Varieties.Preservation][] module of the [Agda Universal Algebra Library][]. In this module we show that identities are preserved by closure operators H, S, and P.  This will establish the easy direction of Birkhoff's HSP Theorem.

<pre class="Agda">

#### <a id="closure-properties">Closure properties</a>

The types defined above represent operators with useful closure properties. We now prove a handful of such properties that we need later.

The next lemma would be too obvious to care about were it not for the fact that we'll need it later, so it too must be formalized.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="S⊆SP"></a><a id="2997" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#2997" class="Function">S⊆SP</a> <a id="3002" class="Symbol">:</a>  <a id="3005" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3006" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#3006" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="3008" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3010" href="Relation.Unary.html#1178" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="3015" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3016" href="Base.Algebras.Basic.html#2774" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="3024" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#2631" class="Generalizable">α</a><a id="3025" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="3027" href="Base.Algebras.Products.html#3097" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="3030" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#2631" class="Generalizable">α</a><a id="3031" class="Symbol">))</a>

 <a id="3964" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#3964" class="Function">lA</a> <a id="3967" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3969" href="Base.Algebras.Basic.html#2774" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="3977" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3978" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#3897" class="Bound">α</a> <a id="3980" href="Agda.Primitive.html#961" class="Primitive Operator">⊔</a> <a id="3982" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#3900" class="Bound">β</a><a id="3983" class="Symbol">)</a>
 <a id="3986" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#3964" class="Function">lA</a> <a id="3989" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="3991" href="Base.Algebras.Basic.html#7180" class="Function">Lift-Alg</a> <a id="4000" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#3914" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="4002" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#3900" class="Bound">β</a>

 <a id="4006" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#4006" class="Function">lAsc</a> <a id="4011" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4013" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#3964" class="Function">lA</a> <a id="4016" href="Base.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#5385" class="Function Operator">IsSubalgebraOfClass</a> <a id="4036" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4037" href="Base.Varieties.Closure.html#4100" class="Datatype">P</a> <a id="4039" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#3903" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="4040" class="Symbol">)</a>
 <a id="4043" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#4006" class="Function">lAsc</a> <a id="4048" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="4050" href="Base.Varieties.Closure.html#10722" class="Function">Lift-Alg-subP&#39;</a> <a id="4065" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4066" href="Base.Varieties.Closure.html#7559" class="Function">S→subalgebra</a><a id="4078" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4079" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#3897" class="Bound">α</a><a id="4080" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="4082" href="Base.Varieties.Closure.html#4100" class="Datatype">P</a><a id="4083" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4084" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#3897" class="Bound">α</a><a id="4085" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="4087" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#3897" class="Bound">α</a><a id="4088" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4090" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#3903" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="4091" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="4093" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#3914" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="4094" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4096" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4097" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#2997" class="Function">S⊆SP</a> <a id="4102" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#3903" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="4104" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#3917" class="Bound">sA</a><a id="4106" class="Symbol">))</a>

 <a id="4111" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#4111" class="Function">lAsp</a> <a id="4116" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4118" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#3964" class="Function">lA</a> <a id="4121" href="Relation.Unary.html#1818" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="4123" href="Base.Varieties.Closure.html#3540" class="Datatype">S</a><a id="4124" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4125" href="Base.Varieties.Closure.html#4100" class="Datatype">P</a> <a id="4127" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#3903" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="4128" class="Symbol">)</a>
 <a id="4131" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#4111" class="Function">lAsp</a> <a id="4136" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="4138" href="Base.Varieties.Closure.html#7192" class="Function">subalgebra→S</a><a id="4150" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4151" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#3897" class="Bound">α</a> <a id="4153" href="Agda.Primitive.html#961" class="Primitive Operator">⊔</a> <a id="4155" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#3900" class="Bound">β</a><a id="4156" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="4158" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#3897" class="Bound">α</a> <a id="4160" href="Agda.Primitive.html#961" class="Primitive Operator">⊔</a> <a id="4162" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#3900" class="Bound">β</a><a id="4163" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="4165" href="Base.Varieties.Closure.html#4100" class="Datatype">P</a><a id="4166" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4167" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#3897" class="Bound">α</a><a id="4168" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="4170" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#3900" class="Bound">β</a><a id="4171" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4173" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#3903" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="4174" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="4176" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#3964" class="Function">lA</a><a id="4178" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4180" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#4006" class="Function">lAsc</a>

 <a id="4187" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#4187" class="Function">lA≅B</a> <a id="4192" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4194" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#3964" class="Function">lA</a> <a id="4197" href="Base.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2018" class="Record Operator">≅</a> <a id="4199" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#3906" class="Bound">𝑩</a>
 <a id="4202" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#4187" class="Function">lA≅B</a> <a id="4207" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="4209" href="Base.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#3057" class="Function">≅-trans</a> <a id="4217" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4218" href="Base.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2968" class="Function">≅-sym</a> <a id="4224" href="Base.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#4417" class="Function">Lift-≅</a><a id="4230" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4232" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#3920" class="Bound">A≅B</a>

</pre>

We need to formalize one more lemma before arriving the main objective of this section, which is the proof of the inclusion PS⊆SP.

</pre>


#### <a id="PS-in-SP">PS(𝒦) ⊆ SP(𝒦)</a>

Finally, we are in a position to prove that a product of subalgebras of algebras
in a class `𝒦` is a subalgebra of a product of algebras in `𝒦`.

#### <a id="more-class-inclusions">More class inclusions</a>

We conclude this subsection with three more inclusion relations that will have
bit parts to play later (e.g., in the formal proof of Birkhoff's Theorem).

<pre class="Agda">

#### <a id="V-is-closed-under-lift">V is closed under lift</a>

As mentioned earlier, a technical hurdle that must be overcome when formalizing
proofs in Agda is the proper handling of universe levels. In particular, in the
proof of the Birkhoff's theorem, for example, we will need to know that if an
algebra `𝑨` belongs to the variety `V 𝒦`, then so does the lift of `𝑨`.  Let
us get the tedious proof of this technical lemma out of the way.

Above we proved that `SP(𝒦) ⊆ V(𝒦)`, and we did so under fairly general
assumptions about the universe level parameters.  Unfortunately, this is sometimes
not quite general enough, so we now prove the inclusion again for the specific
universe parameters that align with subsequent applications of this result.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="8495" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="8502" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#8502" class="Module">_</a>  <a id="8505" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8506" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#8506" class="Bound">α</a> <a id="8508" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8510" href="Agda.Primitive.html#742" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="8515" class="Symbol">}</a>  <a id="8518" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8519" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#8519" class="Bound">fe₀</a> <a id="8523" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8525" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#1239" class="Function">funext</a> <a id="8532" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8533" href="Base.Algebras.Products.html#3097" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="8536" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#8506" class="Bound">α</a><a id="8537" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8539" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#8506" class="Bound">α</a><a id="8540" class="Symbol">}</a>
          <a id="8552" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8553" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#8553" class="Bound">fe₁</a> <a id="8557" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8559" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#1239" class="Function">funext</a> <a id="8566" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="8568" href="Base.Algebras.Products.html#3097" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="8571" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#8506" class="Bound">α</a><a id="8572" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8574" href="Agda.Primitive.html#961" class="Primitive Operator">⊔</a> <a id="8576" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8577" href="Agda.Primitive.html#931" class="Primitive">suc</a> <a id="8581" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8582" href="Base.Algebras.Products.html#3097" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="8585" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#8506" class="Bound">α</a><a id="8586" class="Symbol">)))</a> <a id="8590" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8591" href="Agda.Primitive.html#931" class="Primitive">suc</a> <a id="8595" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8596" href="Base.Algebras.Products.html#3097" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="8599" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#8506" class="Bound">α</a><a id="8600" class="Symbol">))}</a>
          <a id="8614" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8615" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#8615" class="Bound">fe₂</a> <a id="8619" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8621" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#1239" class="Function">funext</a> <a id="8628" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8629" href="Base.Algebras.Products.html#3097" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="8632" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#8506" class="Bound">α</a><a id="8633" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8635" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8636" href="Base.Algebras.Products.html#3097" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="8639" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#8506" class="Bound">α</a><a id="8640" class="Symbol">)}</a>
          <a id="8653" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8654" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#8654" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="8656" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8658" href="Relation.Unary.html#1178" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="8663" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8664" href="Base.Algebras.Basic.html#2774" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="8672" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#8506" class="Bound">α</a><a id="8673" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="8675" href="Base.Algebras.Products.html#3097" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="8678" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#8506" class="Bound">α</a><a id="8679" class="Symbol">)}</a> <a id="8682" class="Keyword">where</a>

 <a id="8774" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#8724" class="Function">SP⊆V&#39;</a> <a id="8780" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8781" href="Base.Varieties.Closure.html#3625" class="InductiveConstructor">sbase</a><a id="8786" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8787" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#8787" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="8788" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="8790" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#8790" class="Bound">x</a><a id="8791" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8793" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="8795" href="Base.Varieties.Closure.html#5716" class="InductiveConstructor">visow</a> <a id="8801" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8802" href="Base.Varieties.Closure.html#11830" class="Function">VlA</a> <a id="8806" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8807" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#7447" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="8812" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8813" href="Base.Varieties.Closure.html#3625" class="InductiveConstructor">sbase</a> <a id="8819" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#8790" class="Bound">x</a><a id="8820" class="Symbol">)))</a> <a id="8824" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8825" href="Base.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2968" class="Function">≅-sym</a> <a id="8831" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8832" href="Base.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#5104" class="Function">Lift-Alg-assoc</a> <a id="8847" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="8849" class="Symbol">_{</a><a id="8851" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#8787" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="8852" class="Symbol">}))</a>
 <a id="8857" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#8724" class="Function">SP⊆V&#39;</a> <a id="8863" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8864" href="Base.Varieties.Closure.html#3679" class="InductiveConstructor">slift</a> <a id="8870" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#8870" class="Bound">x</a><a id="8871" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8873" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="8875" href="Base.Varieties.Closure.html#11830" class="Function">VlA</a> <a id="8879" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8880" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#7447" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="8885" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#8870" class="Bound">x</a><a id="8886" class="Symbol">)</a>

 <a id="8890" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#8724" class="Function">SP⊆V&#39;</a> <a id="8896" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8897" href="Base.Varieties.Closure.html#3741" class="InductiveConstructor">ssub</a><a id="8901" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8902" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#8902" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="8903" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="8905" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#8905" class="Bound">𝑩</a><a id="8906" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="8908" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#8908" class="Bound">spA</a> <a id="8912" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#8912" class="Bound">B≤A</a><a id="8915" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8917" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="8919" href="Base.Varieties.Closure.html#5411" class="InductiveConstructor">vssubw</a> <a id="8926" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8927" href="Base.Varieties.Closure.html#11830" class="Function">VlA</a> <a id="8931" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8932" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#7447" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="8937" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#8908" class="Bound">spA</a><a id="8940" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="8943" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#8959" class="Function">B≤lA</a>
  <a id="8950" class="Keyword">where</a>
   <a id="8959" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#8959" class="Function">B≤lA</a> <a id="8964" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8966" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#8905" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="8968" href="Base.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#1868" class="Function Operator">≤</a> <a id="8970" href="Base.Algebras.Basic.html#7180" class="Function">Lift-Alg</a> <a id="8979" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#8902" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="8981" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8982" href="Agda.Primitive.html#931" class="Primitive">suc</a> <a id="8986" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8987" href="Base.Algebras.Products.html#3097" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="8990" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#8506" class="Bound">α</a><a id="8991" class="Symbol">))</a>
   <a id="8997" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#8959" class="Function">B≤lA</a> <a id="9002" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9004" href="Base.Subalgebras.Properties.html#5604" class="Function">≤-Lift</a> <a id="9011" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#8902" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="9013" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#8912" class="Bound">B≤A</a>

 <a id="9019" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#8724" class="Function">SP⊆V&#39;</a> <a id="9025" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9026" href="Base.Varieties.Closure.html#3815" class="InductiveConstructor">siso</a><a id="9030" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9031" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#9031" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="9032" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="9034" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#9034" class="Bound">𝑩</a><a id="9035" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9037" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#9037" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="9039" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#9039" class="Bound">A≅B</a><a id="9042" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9044" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9046" href="Base.Varieties.Closure.html#5716" class="InductiveConstructor">visow</a> <a id="9052" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9053" href="Base.Varieties.Closure.html#11830" class="Function">VlA</a> <a id="9057" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9058" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#7447" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="9063" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#9037" class="Bound">x</a><a id="9064" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="9067" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#9083" class="Function">Goal</a>
  <a id="9074" class="Keyword">where</a>
   <a id="9083" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#9083" class="Function">Goal</a> <a id="9088" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9090" href="Base.Algebras.Basic.html#7180" class="Function">Lift-Alg</a> <a id="9099" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#9031" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="9101" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9102" href="Agda.Primitive.html#931" class="Primitive">suc</a> <a id="9106" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9107" href="Base.Algebras.Products.html#3097" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="9110" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#8506" class="Bound">α</a><a id="9111" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="9114" href="Base.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2018" class="Record Operator">≅</a> <a id="9116" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#9034" class="Bound">𝑩</a>
   <a id="9121" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#9083" class="Function">Goal</a> <a id="9126" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9128" href="Base.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#3057" class="Function">≅-trans</a> <a id="9136" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9137" href="Base.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2968" class="Function">≅-sym</a> <a id="9143" href="Base.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#4417" class="Function">Lift-≅</a><a id="9149" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9151" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#9039" class="Bound">A≅B</a>
</pre>


#### <a id="S-in-SP">⨅ S(𝒦) ∈ SP(𝒦)</a>

Finally, we prove a result that plays an important role, e.g., in the formal proof
of Birkhoff's Theorem. As we saw in [Base.Algebras.Products][], the (informal)
product `⨅ S(𝒦)` of all subalgebras of algebras in 𝒦 is implemented (formally)
in the [agda-algebras](https://github.com/ualib/agda-algebras) library as
`⨅ 𝔄 S(𝒦)`. Our goal is to prove that this product belongs to `SP(𝒦)`. We do so by
first proving that the product belongs to `PS(𝒦)` and then applying the `PS⊆SP` lemma.

Before doing so, we need to redefine the class product so that each factor comes
with a map from the type `X` of variable symbols into that factor.  We will
explain the reason for this below.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="9902" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="class-products-with-maps"></a><a id="9909" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#9909" class="Module">class-products-with-maps</a> <a id="9934" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9935" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#9935" class="Bound">α</a> <a id="9937" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9939" href="Agda.Primitive.html#742" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="9944" class="Symbol">}</a>
 <a id="9947" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9948" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#9948" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="9950" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9952" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#784" class="Primitive">Type</a> <a id="9957" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#9935" class="Bound">α</a><a id="9958" class="Symbol">}</a>
 <a id="9961" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9962" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#9962" class="Bound">fe𝓕α</a> <a id="9967" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9969" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#1239" class="Function">funext</a> <a id="9976" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9977" href="Base.Algebras.Products.html#3097" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="9980" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#9935" class="Bound">α</a><a id="9981" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9983" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#9935" class="Bound">α</a><a id="9984" class="Symbol">}</a>
 <a id="9987" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9988" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#9988" class="Bound">fe₁</a> <a id="9992" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9994" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#1239" class="Function">funext</a> <a id="10001" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="10003" href="Base.Algebras.Products.html#3097" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="10006" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#9935" class="Bound">α</a><a id="10007" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="10009" href="Agda.Primitive.html#961" class="Primitive Operator">⊔</a> <a id="10011" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10012" href="Agda.Primitive.html#931" class="Primitive">suc</a> <a id="10016" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10017" href="Base.Algebras.Products.html#3097" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="10020" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#9935" class="Bound">α</a><a id="10021" class="Symbol">)))</a> <a id="10025" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10026" href="Agda.Primitive.html#931" class="Primitive">suc</a> <a id="10030" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10031" href="Base.Algebras.Products.html#3097" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="10034" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#9935" class="Bound">α</a><a id="10035" class="Symbol">))}</a>
 <a id="10040" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="10041" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#10041" class="Bound">fe₂</a> <a id="10045" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10047" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#1239" class="Function">funext</a> <a id="10054" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10055" href="Base.Algebras.Products.html#3097" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="10058" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#9935" class="Bound">α</a><a id="10059" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="10061" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10062" href="Base.Algebras.Products.html#3097" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="10065" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#9935" class="Bound">α</a><a id="10066" class="Symbol">)}</a>
 <a id="10070" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10071" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#10071" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="10073" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10075" href="Relation.Unary.html#1178" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="10080" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10081" href="Base.Algebras.Basic.html#2774" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="10089" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#9935" class="Bound">α</a><a id="10090" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="10092" href="Base.Algebras.Products.html#3097" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="10095" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#9935" class="Bound">α</a><a id="10096" class="Symbol">))</a>
 <a id="10100" class="Keyword">where</a>

 <a id="class-products-with-maps.ℑ&#39;"></a><a id="10108" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#10108" class="Function">ℑ&#39;</a> <a id="10111" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10113" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#784" class="Primitive">Type</a> <a id="10118" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10119" href="Base.Algebras.Products.html#3097" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="10122" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#9935" class="Bound">α</a><a id="10123" class="Symbol">)</a>
 <a id="10126" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#10108" class="Function">ℑ&#39;</a> <a id="10129" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="10131" href="Data.Product.Base.html#1244" class="Function">Σ[</a> <a id="10134" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#10134" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="10136" href="Data.Product.Base.html#1244" class="Function">∈</a> <a id="10138" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10139" href="Base.Algebras.Basic.html#2774" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="10147" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#9935" class="Bound">α</a><a id="10148" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="10150" href="Data.Product.Base.html#1244" class="Function">]</a> <a id="10152" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="10154" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#10134" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="10156" href="Relation.Unary.html#1818" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="10158" href="Base.Varieties.Closure.html#3540" class="Datatype">S</a><a id="10159" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="10160" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#9935" class="Bound">α</a><a id="10161" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="10163" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#9935" class="Bound">α</a><a id="10164" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="10166" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#10071" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="10167" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="10169" href="Data.Product.Base.html#1618" class="Function Operator">×</a> <a id="10171" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10172" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#9948" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="10174" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="10176" href="Overture.Basic.html#4325" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="10178" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#10134" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="10180" href="Overture.Basic.html#4325" class="Function Operator">∣</a><a id="10181" class="Symbol">))</a>

</pre>

Notice that the second component of this dependent pair type is
`(𝑨 ∈ 𝒦) × (X → ∣ 𝑨 ∣)`. In previous versions of the [UALib][] this second
component was simply `𝑨 ∈ 𝒦`, until we realized that adding the type `X → ∣ 𝑨 ∣`
is quite useful. Later we will see exactly why, but for now suffice it to say that
a map of type `X → ∣ 𝑨 ∣` may be viewed abstractly as an *ambient context*, or
more concretely, as an assignment of *values* in `∣ 𝑨 ∣` to *variable symbols* in
`X`.  When computing with or reasoning about products, while we don't want to
rigidly impose a context in advance, want do want to lay our hands on whatever
context is ultimately assumed.  Including the "context map" inside the index type
`ℑ` of the product turns out to be a convenient way to achieve this flexibility.


Taking the product over the index type `ℑ` requires a function that maps an index
`i : ℑ` to the corresponding algebra.  Each `i : ℑ` is a triple, say,
`(𝑨 , p , h)`, where `𝑨 : Algebra α`, `p : 𝑨 ∈ 𝒦`, and `h : X → ∣ 𝑨 ∣`, so the
function mapping an index to the corresponding algebra is simply the first projection.

<pre class="Agda">

 <a id="class-products-with-maps.𝔄&#39;"></a><a id="11317" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#11317" class="Function">𝔄&#39;</a> <a id="11320" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11322" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#10108" class="Function">ℑ&#39;</a> <a id="11325" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="11327" href="Base.Algebras.Basic.html#2774" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="11335" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#9935" class="Bound">α</a>
 <a id="11338" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#11317" class="Function">𝔄&#39;</a> <a id="11341" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="11343" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="11345" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11346" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#11346" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="11348" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11350" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#10108" class="Function">ℑ&#39;</a><a id="11352" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="11354" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="11356" href="Overture.Basic.html#4325" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="11358" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#11346" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="11360" href="Overture.Basic.html#4325" class="Function Operator">∣</a>

</pre>

Finally, we define `class-product` which represents the product of all members of
`𝒦`.

<pre class="Agda">

 <a id="class-products-with-maps.class-product&#39;"></a><a id="11478" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#11478" class="Function">class-product&#39;</a> <a id="11493" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11495" href="Base.Algebras.Basic.html#2774" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="11503" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11504" href="Base.Algebras.Products.html#3097" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="11507" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#9935" class="Bound">α</a><a id="11508" class="Symbol">)</a>
 <a id="11511" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#11478" class="Function">class-product&#39;</a> <a id="11526" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="11528" href="Base.Algebras.Products.html#1923" class="Function">⨅</a> <a id="11530" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#11317" class="Function">𝔄&#39;</a>

</pre>

If `p : 𝑨 ∈ 𝒦` and `h : X → ∣ 𝑨 ∣`, we view the triple `(𝑨 , p , h) ∈ ℑ` as an
index over the class, and so we can think of `𝔄 (𝑨 , p , h)` (which is simply `𝑨`)
as the projection of the product `⨅ 𝔄` onto the `(𝑨 , p, h)`-th component.

<pre class="Agda">

 <a id="class-products-with-maps.class-prod-s-∈-ps"></a><a id="11799" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#11799" class="Function">class-prod-s-∈-ps</a> <a id="11817" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11819" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#11478" class="Function">class-product&#39;</a> <a id="11834" href="Relation.Unary.html#1818" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="11836" href="Base.Varieties.Closure.html#4100" class="Datatype">P</a><a id="11837" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="11838" href="Base.Algebras.Products.html#3097" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="11841" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#9935" class="Bound">α</a><a id="11842" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="11844" href="Base.Algebras.Products.html#3097" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="11847" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#9935" class="Bound">α</a><a id="11848" class="Symbol">}(</a><a id="11850" href="Base.Varieties.Closure.html#3540" class="Datatype">S</a> <a id="11852" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#10071" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="11853" class="Symbol">)</a>
 <a id="11856" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#11799" class="Function">class-prod-s-∈-ps</a> <a id="11874" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="11876" href="Base.Varieties.Closure.html#4544" class="InductiveConstructor">pisow</a> <a id="11882" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#12154" class="Function">psPllA</a> <a id="11889" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11890" href="Base.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#5693" class="Function">⨅≅</a> <a id="11893" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="11894" class="Argument">fiu</a> <a id="11898" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="11900" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#10041" class="Bound">fe₂</a><a id="11903" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="11905" class="Argument">fiw</a> <a id="11909" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="11911" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#9962" class="Bound">fe𝓕α</a><a id="11915" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="11917" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#12205" class="Function">llA≅A</a><a id="11922" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="11926" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="11934" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#11934" class="Function">lA</a> <a id="11937" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#11937" class="Function">llA</a> <a id="11941" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11943" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#10108" class="Function">ℑ&#39;</a> <a id="11946" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="11948" href="Base.Algebras.Basic.html#2774" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="11956" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11957" href="Base.Algebras.Products.html#3097" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="11960" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#9935" class="Bound">α</a><a id="11961" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="12154" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#12154" class="Function">psPllA</a> <a id="12161" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12163" href="Base.Algebras.Products.html#1923" class="Function">⨅</a> <a id="12165" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#11937" class="Function">llA</a> <a id="12169" href="Relation.Unary.html#1818" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="12171" href="Base.Varieties.Closure.html#4100" class="Datatype">P</a> <a id="12173" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12174" href="Base.Varieties.Closure.html#3540" class="Datatype">S</a> <a id="12176" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#10071" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="12177" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="12205" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#12205" class="Function">llA≅A</a> <a id="12211" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12213" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="12215" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#12215" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="12217" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="12219" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12220" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#11937" class="Function">llA</a> <a id="12224" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#12215" class="Bound">i</a><a id="12225" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="12227" href="Base.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2018" class="Record Operator">≅</a> <a id="12229" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12230" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#11317" class="Function">𝔄&#39;</a> <a id="12233" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#12215" class="Bound">i</a><a id="12234" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="12238" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#12205" class="Function">llA≅A</a> <a id="12244" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#12244" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="12246" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="12248" href="Base.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#3057" class="Function">≅-trans</a> <a id="12256" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12257" href="Base.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2968" class="Function">≅-sym</a> <a id="12263" href="Base.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#4417" class="Function">Lift-≅</a><a id="12269" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="12271" href="Base.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2968" class="Function">≅-sym</a> <a id="12277" href="Base.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#4417" class="Function">Lift-≅</a><a id="12283" class="Symbol">)</a>

</pre>


So, since `PS⊆SP`, we see that that the product of all subalgebras of a class `𝒦`
belongs to `SP(𝒦)`.

<pre class="Agda">

 <a id="class-products-with-maps.class-prod-s-∈-sp"></a><a id="12417" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#12417" class="Function">class-prod-s-∈-sp</a> <a id="12435" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12437" href="Base.Equality.Truncation.html#3945" class="Function">hfunext</a> <a id="12445" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12446" href="Base.Algebras.Products.html#3097" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="12449" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#9935" class="Bound">α</a><a id="12450" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="12452" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12453" href="Base.Algebras.Products.html#3097" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="12456" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#9935" class="Bound">α</a><a id="12457" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="12459" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="12461" href="Base.Algebras.Products.html#5383" class="Function">class-product</a> <a id="12475" href="Relation.Unary.html#1818" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="12477" href="Base.Varieties.Closure.html#3540" class="Datatype">S</a><a id="12478" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12479" href="Base.Varieties.Closure.html#4100" class="Datatype">P</a> <a id="12481" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#10071" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="12482" class="Symbol">)</a>
 <a id="12485" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#12417" class="Function">class-prod-s-∈-sp</a> <a id="12503" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#12503" class="Bound">hfe</a> <a id="12507" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="12509" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#5770" class="Function">PS⊆SP</a> <a id="12515" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="12516" class="Argument">fovu</a> <a id="12521" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="12523" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#10041" class="Bound">fe₂</a><a id="12526" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="12528" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#12503" class="Bound">hfe</a> <a id="12532" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#11799" class="Function">class-prod-s-∈-ps</a>
</pre>


#### <a id="h-preserves-identities">H preserves identities</a>

First we prove that the closure operator `H` is compatible with identities that
hold in the given class.

<pre class="Agda">

          <a id="13624" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13625" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#13014" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="13627" href="Base.Terms.Operations.html#2603" class="Function Operator">⟦</a> <a id="13629" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#12993" class="Bound">q</a> <a id="13631" href="Base.Terms.Operations.html#2603" class="Function Operator">⟧</a><a id="13632" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="13634" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#13036" class="Bound">b</a>           <a id="13646" href="Relation.Binary.Reasoning.Syntax.html#12345" class="Function Operator">∎</a>

</pre>

The converse of the foregoing result is almost too obvious to bother with.
Nonetheless, we formalize it for completeness.

<pre class="Agda">

 <a id="13799" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#13799" class="Function">H-id2</a> <a id="13805" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13807" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="13809" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="13810" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#13810" class="Bound">β</a><a id="13811" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="13813" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="13815" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13816" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#13816" class="Bound">p</a> <a id="13818" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#13818" class="Bound">q</a> <a id="13820" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13822" href="Base.Terms.Basic.html#2087" class="Datatype">Term</a> <a id="13827" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#12828" class="Bound">X</a><a id="13828" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="13830" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="13832" href="Base.Varieties.Closure.html#3112" class="Datatype">H</a><a id="13833" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="13834" class="Argument">β</a> <a id="13836" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="13838" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#13810" class="Bound">β</a><a id="13839" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="13841" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#12841" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="13843" href="Base.Varieties.EquationalLogic.html#2528" class="Function Operator">⊫</a> <a id="13845" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#13816" class="Bound">p</a> <a id="13847" href="Base.Varieties.EquationalLogic.html#2528" class="Function Operator">≈</a> <a id="13849" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#13818" class="Bound">q</a> <a id="13851" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="13853" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#12841" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="13855" href="Base.Varieties.EquationalLogic.html#2528" class="Function Operator">⊫</a> <a id="13857" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#13816" class="Bound">p</a> <a id="13859" href="Base.Varieties.EquationalLogic.html#2528" class="Function Operator">≈</a> <a id="13861" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#13818" class="Bound">q</a>

Again, the obvious converse is barely worth the bits needed to formalize it.

and conversely,

 <a id="15862" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#15862" class="Function">P-id2</a> <a id="15868" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15870" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="15872" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="15873" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#15873" class="Bound">β</a><a id="15874" class="Symbol">}(</a><a id="15876" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#15876" class="Bound">p</a> <a id="15878" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#15878" class="Bound">q</a> <a id="15880" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15882" href="Base.Terms.Basic.html#2087" class="Datatype">Term</a> <a id="15887" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#15813" class="Bound">X</a><a id="15888" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="15890" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="15892" href="Base.Varieties.Closure.html#4100" class="Datatype">P</a><a id="15893" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="15894" class="Argument">β</a> <a id="15896" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="15898" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#15873" class="Bound">β</a><a id="15899" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="15901" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#15826" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="15903" href="Base.Varieties.EquationalLogic.html#2528" class="Function Operator">⊫</a> <a id="15905" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#15876" class="Bound">p</a> <a id="15907" href="Base.Varieties.EquationalLogic.html#2528" class="Function Operator">≈</a> <a id="15909" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#15878" class="Bound">q</a> <a id="15911" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="15913" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#15826" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="15915" href="Base.Varieties.EquationalLogic.html#2528" class="Function Operator">⊫</a> <a id="15917" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#15876" class="Bound">p</a> <a id="15919" href="Base.Varieties.EquationalLogic.html#2528" class="Function Operator">≈</a> <a id="15921" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#15878" class="Bound">q</a>

</pre>

#### <a id="v-preserves-identities">V preserves identities</a>

Finally, we prove the analogous preservation lemmas for the closure operator `V`.

</pre>


#### <a id="class-identities">Class identities</a>

From `V-id1` it follows that if 𝒦 is a class of structures, then the set of
identities modeled by all structures in `𝒦` is equivalent to the set of identities
modeled by all structures in `V 𝒦`.  In other terms, `Th (V 𝒦)` is precisely the
set of identities modeled by `𝒦`.   We formalize this observation as follows.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="19655" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="19662" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#19662" class="Module">_</a>  <a id="19665" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19666" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#19666" class="Bound">fe</a> <a id="19669" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19671" href="Base.Equality.Extensionality.html#2206" class="Function">DFunExt</a><a id="19678" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="19680" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#19680" class="Bound">wd</a> <a id="19683" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19685" href="Base.Equality.Welldefined.html#2798" class="Function">SwellDef</a><a id="19693" class="Symbol">)</a>
          <a id="19705" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19706" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#19706" class="Bound">𝓧</a> <a id="19708" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19710" href="Agda.Primitive.html#742" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="19715" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="19717" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#19717" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="19719" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19721" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#784" class="Primitive">Type</a> <a id="19726" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#19706" class="Bound">𝓧</a><a id="19727" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="19729" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19730" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#19730" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="19732" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19734" href="Relation.Unary.html#1178" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="19739" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19740" href="Base.Algebras.Basic.html#2774" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="19748" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#2631" class="Generalizable">α</a><a id="19749" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="19751" href="Base.Algebras.Products.html#3097" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="19754" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#2631" class="Generalizable">α</a><a id="19755" class="Symbol">)}</a> <a id="19758" class="Keyword">where</a>
 <a id="19765" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#19765" class="Function">ovu</a> <a id="19769" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#19769" class="Function">lovu</a> <a id="19774" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19776" href="Agda.Primitive.html#742" class="Postulate">Level</a>
 <a id="19783" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#19765" class="Function">ovu</a> <a id="19787" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="19789" href="Base.Algebras.Products.html#3097" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="19792" href="Base.Varieties.Preservation.html#19748" class="Bound">α</a>

Once again, and for the last time, completeness dictates that we formalize the
coverse of `V-id1`, however obvious it may be.
